It also dropped them into a fourth-place GNAC tie with Montana State Billings. &#10;   &#10;Free throws, as they had been in last Saturday night’s loss at first-place Western Washington and again Thursday, loomed large. &#10;   &#10;While Central made 4 of 12, the Wolves (8-4, 11-9) were 24 of 31. &#10;   &#10;Coach Greg Sparling calculated that over his team’s three-game losing streak the Wildcats have been outscored 73-24 from the free throw line. &#10;   &#10;“I’m not blaming the officials, not at all,” he said. “But the thing is, we simply have got to find a way to get to the foul line more.” &#10;   &#10;Center Fuquan Niles was Central’s lone double-digit scorer, and he posted a double-double with 12 points and 11 rebounds. &#10;   &#10;But Dom Hunter, the GNAC’s scoring leader at 25.2 points per game, managed only nine on 4-of-17 shooting, and the team’s second-leading scorer, Naim Ladd, sat out with an injury sustained late in Thursday’s game. &#10;   &#10;Ali Faruq-Bey led Western Oregon with 21 points and Demetrius Trammell, a transfer from Yakima Valley College, had 12 off the bench. &#10;   &#10;“We have 72 hours before we take a seven-hour bus ride to Northwest Nazarene,” Sparling said, “and we’ve got to get a lot of things fixed.” &#10;   &#10;WESTERN OREGON — Ali Faruq-Bey 6-12 4-4 21, JJ Chirnside 4-9 2-5 13, Evan Garrison 3-4 6-6 10, Tanner Omlid 4-10 0-0 10, Reese 2-6 5-6 9, Demetrius Trammell 4-7 3-4 12, Leaks 2-3 2-2 8, Edwards 0-2 1-2 1, Souza 0-0 1-2 1, Thompson 0-0 0-0 0, Berg 0-0 0-0 0.
